 aspx India dismissed Pakistan's allegations of supporting espionage and terrorist activities against eight Indian High Commission officials in Islamabad, terming them 'baseless and unconfirmed'
 in aaropon ke kaaran bharat ke paas apane in adhikariyon ko waapas bulaane ke alaava koi anya vikalp nahin bachaa he
 Foreign Ministry spokesperson Vikas Swaroop said in a sharp response that the charges against the Indian authorities were later fabricated and it was a 'rude attempt' to target them, despite no fault of theirs
 isse pehle pakistan ucchayog ke ek sadsy ko pichley hafte bharat virdohi gatividhiyon main shaamil hone par range haath pakadaa gaya tha
 India has also strongly protested the manner in which the names and photos of eight Indian officials were printed and their security compromised
 inamen se chaar adhikariyon ke paas rajanyik passport he
 Pakistan claimed that Indian High Commission officials were involved in activities such as espionage, subversive and terrorist activities in Balochistan and Sindh, especially Karachi, damaging the china-pakistan economic circuit and fueling instability in both states
 yah puche jane par ki kya bhartiya adhikariyon ko waapas bulaayaa ja rahaa he, swaroop ne kaha ki yah ek prakriyaagat maamla he tathaa sarkaar sthiti ke sabhi pahaluon ko dhyaan main rakhkar aavashyak kadam uthaaegi
 He called security a priority
 swaroop ne kaha, 'ham pakistan dwaara islamabad main bhartiya ucchayog ke kuch adhikariyon ke khilaaf lagaae gaye niraadhaar or bina pushtiwale aaropon ko puri tarah khaarij karte hai
 The government completely denies these allegations
 ' unhone kaha, 'yah visheshrup se khedjanak he ki pakistani adhikariyon ne apane chah adhikariyon ko paak ucchayog se waapas bulaane ke baad yah aarope lagaana pasand kiya
 Some of these officers were named by Mahmud Akhtar before the Indian authorities
 akhtar pakistan ucchayog kaa vah adhikari he, jise range haath pakadaa gaya tha
 ' pataa chalaa he ki bharat aath rajanyikon ko waapas bulaaegaa kyonki unki suraksha ke saath samjhauta kiya gaya he
 Swaroop said that the 'wrongly implicated' Indian officials were working towards increasing trade and economic contacts between the people and between the two countries
 unhone kaha, 'unke khilaaf pakistan ke galat aaropon ke kaaran ucchayog kii sambhddha gatividhiyon par pratikul prabhaav padane kii ashanka he
 He said the government strongly opposed the manner in which the names and photographs of eight Indians were printed, of which four have diplomatic passports
 yah rajanyik chalan evam shishtachar ke moolbhoot niyamon ke viruddh he
 a spokesman for the Ministry of External Affairs said that the allegations against Indian officials are harmful to their security
 swaroop ne kaha, 'ham ummid karte hai ki pakistan kii sarkaar na keval in aath rajanyikon evam adhikariyon balki ucchayog ke anya sadasyon evam unke pariwaron ke pakistan main rahane ke dauraan unki suraksha sunishchit karne ke liye sabhi aavashyak kadam uthaaegi
 Comments pakistan ne apane ucchayog ke karmchaariyon ke ek jasusi cond main sanliptata ke bich apane chah adhikariyon ko waapas bula liya tha
 Pakistan had last week declared Officer Surjit Singh at the Indian High Commission as an unwanted person and Swaroop said that Singh was recalled
 swaroop ne kaha ki pakistan ke niraadhaar aaropon ke kaaran kshetra kii shanti or suraksha ke liye jokhim bad gaya he, jo padosiyon ke khilaaf seemaa paar aatankwaad ko pakistan dwaara diye jane vaale sahyog ke kaaran hi paidaa hua he
 He said that Pakistan completely denies the problem and shuns its responsibilities by making unwarranted allegations
 (hedline ke alaava, is khabar ko enditivi team ne sampadit nahin kiya he, yah syndicate feed se sidhe prakashit kii gai he
 ) videsh mantralay ke pravaktaa vikaas swaroop ne tikhi pratikriya main kaha ki bhartiya adhikariyon ke khilaaf aarope baad main gadhakar lagaae gaye or unki koi galati nahin hone ke baavjood unhen nishaanaa banane kaa yah ek 'ashisht prayaas' he
 Earlier, a member of the Pakistan High Commission was caught red-handed last week for his involvement in anti-india activities
 bharat ne us tareeke par bhi kadaa virodh jataayaa he, jisamen aath bhartiya adhikariyon ke naam or photo ko chapa gaya or unki suraksha se samjhauta kiya gaya
 Four of these officers hold diplomatic passports
 pakistan ne daawa kiya ki bhartiya ucchayog ke adhikari baluchistan or sindh khaskar karachi main jasusi, vidhvansak or aatanki gatividhiyon ko sahyog dene, china pakistan aarthik paripath ko nuksaan pahunchane evam donon rajyon main asthirataa ko hawa dene jaise kaaryon main sanlipt the
 Asked whether the Indian authorities were being called back, Swaroop said that this is a procedural matter and the government will take necessary steps keeping all aspects of the situation in mind
 unhone suraksha ko ek praathamikta bataaya
 Swaroop said, "we completely reject the baseless and unconfirmed allegations made by Pakistan against some officials of the Indian High Commission in Islamabad
" sarkaar in aaropon se puri tarah inkaar karti he
 He said, "it is particularly regrettable that the Pakistani authorities preferred to make the allegations after recalling six of their officers from the Pakistan High Commission
" in adhikariyon main se kuch ke naam mahmud akhtar ne bhartiya adhikariyon ke samaksh liye the
 Akhtar is the officer of Pakistan High Commission who was caught red handed
 ' It is learned that India will call back eight diplomats as their security is compromised
 swaroop ne kaha ki 'galat rup se fansaae gaye' bhartiya adhikari donon deshon ke bich logon ke madhya tathaa vyapaar evam aarthik sampark badhaane kii disha main kaam kar rahe the
 He said, "allied activities of the High Commission are feared to be adversely affected by Pakistan's false allegations against them
" ' unhone kaha ki sarkaar us tareeke kaa kadai se virodh karti he jisamen aath bharatiyon ke naam evam photo chaape gaye jinamein se chaar ke paas rajanyik passport he
 This is against the fundamental rules of diplomatic practice and etiquette
 videsh mantralay ke pravaktaa ne kaha ki bhartiya adhikariyon ke khilaaf aarope unki suraksha ke prati hanikaarak hai
 Swaroop said, 'we hope that the Government of Pakistan will take all necessary steps to ensure the safety of not only these eight diplomats and officials but also other members of the High Commission and their families during their stay in Pakistan
 'tippaniyan Pakistan had withdrawn six of its officers amid involvement in a spy scandal by its High Commission staff
 pakistan ne pichley saptaah bhartiya ucchayog main adhikari surajeet singh ko avaanchit vyakti ghoshit kiya tha tathaa swaroop ne bataaya ki singh ko waapas bula liya gaya
 Swaroop said that Pakistan's baseless allegations have increased the risk to the peace and security of the region, which has arisen due to Pakistan's support to cross-border terrorism against neighbors

 Ramzan 2019: The month of Ramadan is very important for every Muslim, in which fasting is kept for 30 days
 islam ke mutabik, puure ramajaan ko teen hisson main baanta gaya he, jo pehla, doosraa or teesraa ashara kehalaata he
 Ashara is Arabic's number 10
 is tarah ramajaan ke pehle 10 din (1-10) main pehla ashara, duusare 10 din (11-20) main doosraa ashara or tisare din (21-30) main teesraa ashara banta hota he
 In this way there are 3 Ashes in the month of Ramadan
 pehla ashara rahamat kaa hota he, doosraa ashara magafirat yani gunahon kii maafee kaa hota he or teesraa ashara jahannam (hell) kii aag se khud ko bachaane ke liye hota he
 Prophet Mohammad has said about the month of Ramadan, there is mercy in the beginning of Ramadan, in the middle there is Magafirat i
e
 forgiveness and at the end there is protection from the fire of Jahannam (hell)
 ramajaan ke shuruaati 10 dinon main rojaa-namaaj karne waalon par allaah kii rahamat hoti he
 Muslims can be sanctified by their sins during Ramadan, i
e
 in the second asylum
 vahiin, ramajaan ke aakhri yani tisare ashare main jahannam kii aag se khud ko bachaa sakate hai
 3 Ashes of Ramadan and their importance - 1
 ramajaan kaa pehla ashara (first Stage of Ramadan- 'mercy')-ramajaan maheene ke pehle 10 din rahamat ke hote hai
 Allah blesses those who offer Rosa prayers
 ramajaan ke pehle ashare main musalamaanon ko zyada se zyada daan kar ke garibon kii madad kerani chahie
 Every human should be treated with love and gentleness
 2
 Second Stage of Ramadan- 'forgiveness' - The second Ashra runs from the 11th day of Ramadan to the 20th day
 yah ashara maafee kaa hota he
 People can get forgiveness from their sins by praying in this shelter
 islamic manyata ke mutabik, agar koi insaan ramajaan ke duusare ashare main apane gunahon (paapon) se maafee maangata he, to duusare dinon ke mukaable is samay allaah apane bandon ko jaldi maaf karata he
 3
 ramajaan kaa teesraa ashara (third Stage of Ramadan 'nijat')-ramajaan kaa teesraa or aakhri ashara 21wein roje se shuru hokar chand ke hisaab se 29wein yaa 30wein roje tak chalata he
 This ashra is considered the most important
 tisare ashare kaa uddeshy jahannam (hell) kii aag se khud ko surakshit rakhana he
 During this time, every Muslim should pray to Allah to avoid Jahannam
 ramajaan ke aakhri ashare main kai muslim mard or auraten ehtakaaf main baithte hai
 Let me tell you, in Ehtakaf, Muslim men sit in a corner of the mosque for 10 days and pray to Allah, while women pray at home only

 *** Union Finance Minister Pranab Mukherjee met Congress President Sonia Gandhi on Thursday
 adhikariyon ne bataaya ki donon netaaon ke bich aagaamee raashtrapati chunaavon ko lekar charchaa hui
 Pranab reached Sonia's 10, Janpath residence around 10 am
 pashchim bengal kii mukhyamantri mamata banerjee va samaajawaadee party (sapa) pramukh mulaayam singh yadav dwaara pranab ko raashtrapati va hamid ansaari ko up raashtrapati banaae jane ke sonia ke faisle ko lagbhag asweekaar kar die jane ke baad donon netaaon ke bich yah mulaakaat hui
 Mamta and Mulayam as their presidential candidates, Prime Minister Manmohan Singh, former President A
K
 pi
 J
 abdul kalam or purv loksabhaa adhyaksh somnath chatarji kaa naam sujhaayaa he

 ke
 Antony, Home Minister p Chidambaram and Energy Minister Sushil Kumar Shinde met Sonia separately
 vahiin upie kii ghatak dal dramuk netaa tii aar baaluu ne sonia gandhi se mulaakaat ke baad kaha ki samprag kii ore se raashtrapati ummidavaar ke naam kii jald ghoshnaa karengi sonia
 Other constituents of the UPA, National Conference and Rashtriya Lok Dal have spoken of supporting the presidential candidate of Congress
 vahiin lalu prasad yadav, ramvilas paswan ne kaha he ki upie ke ummidavaar ko unka samarthan hasil hoga
 Rajasthan Royals captain Rahul Dravid today praised Shane Watson, saying that he is a true match winner and his innings of 70 off 34 balls is one of the best innings
 watasan ne chennai super kings ke gendbaajon kii dhajjiyaan udaate hue ravivaar ko rajasthan royles ko paanch wicket se jeet dilaai
 The comments dravid ne match ke baad kaha, hamen ummid thi ki vah aisi pari khelegaa, kyonki vah sahi myne main match vinar he, jis tarah se usne aswin ke over main dhuandhar ballebaaji karke dabaav hataaya, vah sarvshereshth ballebaaji kaa namoona tha
 We had lost four wickets for 45 runs, but then changed the match map by playing innings like David Miller
 kings ilevan punjab ke miller ne royal chalangers bengalooru ke khilaaf 38 gend main 101 ran banaakar team ko jeet dilaai thi
 Dravid also praised Stuart Binny for scoring an unbeaten 41
 unhone kaha, binni ab kaaphi behatar cricketer ho gaya he, jis tarah se usne dabaav kaa saamana kiya, usase uski paripakvata najar ai
 Now national selectors should also pay attention to this
 tii-20 cricket main vah behtareen finishr he
 Watson blasted the Chennai Super Kings bowlers to win the Rajasthan Royals by five wickets on Sunday
 tippaniyan Dravid said after the match, "we expected him to play such an innings, because he is a true match winner, the way he took the pressure off the batting in Ashwin's over, he was the best batting model
" hamane chaar wicket 45 ran par ganvaa die the, lekin phir usne david miller jaisi pari khelkar match kaa nakshaa badal diya
 Miller of Kings XI Punjab won the team against Royal Challengers Bangalore by scoring 101 runs off 38 balls
 dravid ne naabad 41 ran banane vaale stuart binni kii bhi tarif kii

 ab rashtriya chayankartaaon ko bhi is par dhyaan dena chahie

 The tourism industry of the state has got a boost with the one-month Rann Utsav (marumohotsav) in Kutch district of Gujarat
 is baar yah utsav 19 disambar ko shuru hua tha
 Gujarat Tourism Minister Jaynarayan Vyas said, there has been a big improvement in the tourism sector of the state in the last three years
 is dauraan joardaar prachaar abhiyaan se rajya main paryatakon kii aavak 70 fisad tak badi he
 He said that the growth of Amitabh Bachchan as brand ambassador by Gujarat Tourism has also boosted tourism
 unhone kaha ki ran utsav pichley teen saal se manaaya ja rahaa he par yah is baar puure ek maheene chalaaya gaya
 This led to a boom in tourism
 teen saal pehle yahaan baahar se 725 paryatak aae
 This time the number has increased to 30,000
 aam aadmi party ke vidhayak amanatulla khan kaa party se nilabann somvaar ko radd kar diya gaya
 It has been said that the senior leader of the AAP was instrumental in getting Amanatullah suspended
 lekin amanatulla ne kumaar vishwaas se kisi tarah kii anban se saaf inkaar kiya he
 Amanatullah Khan, MLA from Okhla in South Delhi, told Aaj Tak, "I got a call from party leader Ashutosh that your suspension is withdrawn
" meraa kumaar vishwaas se na aamanaa saamana hua na kabhi baatcheet hui
 Kumar Vishwas is the senior leader
 us vakt unki naaraazgi dur karne arvind gaye the, kyonki party ko baandhe rakhane mukhiya kii jimmedaari he
 "the suspension canceled in the wake of the passing election," he said, "being unable to participate in party activities due to being out of the party
" abhigujrat or uttar pradesh main chunaavhai jahaan meri jarurat samajhi gayi he
 The party will take the decision to return to the Political Affairs Committee (PAC)
 maine apane bayaan par kamity ko likhit main jawaab de diya he
 The party mlas are together at the moment, the entire party is united with Arvind Kejriwal
 is vakt sabhi ko party ke liye kaam karnaa chahie
 "amanatullah Khan may be denying that he was angry with Kumar Vishwas today, but when he was suspended, he made three big allegations against Kumar Vishwas in conversation with Aaj Tak
 is bayaan par hua tha vivadjis bayaan se vivaad khadaa hua tha usamen amanatulla khan ne kumaar vishwaas par bijepi ke ishaare par chalane kaa aarope lagaate hue kaha tha ki 'kumaravishwaas AAP ko hadapna chaahtehain or todna chaahate hai
 Kumar is calling the mlas in his house and saying that make me the convener of the party, or else go to BJP
 bijepi har ek ko 30 karod dene ke liye taiyaar he'
 Amanatullah Khan had made a serious allegation of breaking the party on Vishwas that he feels that all this is happening at the behest of BJP and BJP has left 4 mlas for this work
 bijepi ke ye chaaron vidhayak AAP ke vidhayakon ko kumaar vishwaas ke ghar le jate hai, is baat kii tasdik AAP ke tamaam vidhayakon ne kii
 The dispute between Delhi Chief Minister Arvind Kejriwal and Lieutenant Governor Najeeb Jung reached President Pranab Mukherjee
 donon ne ek duusare par samvidhan kaa ulanghan karne or apane apane adhikaar kshetra se aage jaakar kadam uthaane ke aarope lagaae
 a few hours before Kejriwal met the President, Jung met Mukherjee and apprised him of the ongoing confrontation over the appointment of key officers in the Delhi government
 sutron ke mutabik kaha gaya ki dilli main sanvaidhanik sankat jaise halaat hai
 The Lt
 Governor says that he has the right to appoint and transfer officers and none of his actions are as 'unconstitutional' as the AAP government is alleging
 iske baad kejariwal ne raashtrapati dwaara die gaye samay ke anusaar unase mulaakaat kii
 He was accompanied by Deputy Chief Minister Manish Sisodia, who said, 'the Lieutenant Governor is acting as if the national capital is under President's rule and there is no elected government here
 ' Sisodia told reporters after meeting Mukherjee, "despite having a democratically elected government, the Lieutenant Governor is ignoring the Chief Minister and ministers and issuing instructions to the officials
 agar adhikari unke aadesh kaa paalan nahin karte to vah unhen tabadale kii dhamkee tak de rahe hai
 This is not good for democracy
 ' Sisodia said, 'we told the President that we accepted the Lt
 Governor's decision to appoint the Acting Chief Secretary without consulting each other
 lekin vah uske baad bhi nirvaachit sarkaar kii andekhi kar adhikariyon kii niyukti kar rahe hai
 He is even interfering with the appointments of secretaries and directly ordering them
 to loktantr kahaan he
 ' vahiin uparajyapal najeeb jang ne isse pehle din main grahamantri rajnath singh se bhi is mudde par mulaakaat kii thi or aap sarkaar ke saath unke gatirodh ke bare main jaankaree di thi
 The conflict between the AAP government and the war has intensified over the appointment of Shakuntala Gamlin as Acting Chief Secretary of Delhi
 kejariwal kaa aarope he ki uparajyapal prashasan ko apane kabje main lene kaa prayaas kar rahe hai
 Despite Kejriwal's strong opposition, Jung on Friday appointed Gamlin to the post
 sisodiya ne mukherjee ke saath mulaakaat ko acha bataate hue kaha, 'hamane unase anurodh kiya ki uparajyapal se kahen ki vah jo kar rahe hai, nahin karen
 The President listened carefully to us and i hope he will look into the matter
 ' unhone kaha, 'hamane raashtrapati ko bataaya ki uparajyapal is tarah se kaam kar rahe hai, jaise ki dilli main raashtrapati shashan lagu ho
 The main thing is that he is directing the officers directly
 pichley ek hafte main unhone kam se kam chaar baar mukhyamantri, mantriyon, mantriparishad kii andekhi kar sidhe afasaron ko aadesh die hai
 ' isse pehle aap sarkaar ne aaj uparajyapal kii andekhi karte hue varisht adhikari arvind raay ko saamaanya prashasan vibhaag kaa pradhan sachiv niyukt kiya
 It is worth noting that the order for appointment of Rai was issued by Rajendra Kumar as Principal Secretary (services), while Jung declared the appointment of Kumar to the post by the AAP government as ineffective
 aap sarkaar ne anindo majumdaar se saamaanya prashasan vibhaag or seva vibhaag kii jimmedaari lekar kumaar ko saunpi thi
 Majumdar was removed on Saturday as he issued an order on Friday notifying the appointment of Shakuntala Gamlin as acting chief secretary
 usee din shaam ko uparajyapal ne majumdaar ke sthanantaran ko 'nishprabhavi' ghoshit kiya tha
 The comments majumdaar somvaar ko jab dilli sachivalay main apane daftar pahunche the to vahaan taala lataka hua tha
 Later, the AAP government appointed Kumar to the post of Principal Secretary, Department of Services and General Administration
 aap sarkaar ne aaj apane aadesh main kaha ki raay ko rajendra kumaar kii jagah pradhan sachiv niyukt kiya gaya he
 Earlier this year, the AAP government removed Rai from the post of Principal Secretary, Home Department and has not been given any responsibility since then
 kejariwal kii raashtrapati se mulaakaat se kuch ghante pehle jang ne mukherjee se mulaakaat kii or unhen dilli sarkaar main pramukh adhikariyon kii niyukti ko lekar chal rahe takaraav se avgat karaayaa
 According to sources, it was said that there are situations like constitutional crisis in Delhi
 uparajyapal kaa kahana he ki unhen adhikariyon kii niyukti or tabadale kaa adhikaar he or unki koi bhi karrwai 'asanvaidhanik' nahin he jaisaa ki aap sarkaar aarope laga rahi he
 Kejriwal then met him as per the time given by the President
 unke saath up mukhyamantri manish sisodiya bhi the, jinhone kaha, 'uparajyapal is tarah kaam kar rahe hai jaise ki rashtriya rajdhani main raashtrapati shashan laga ho or yahaan koi chuni hui sarkaar nahin ho
 ' sisodiya ne mukherjee se mulaakaat ke baad samvaadadaataaon se kaha, 'loktantric tareeke se chuni hui sarkaar hone ke baavjood uparajyapal mukhyamantri or mantriyon kii andekhi kar rahe hai or adhikariyon ko nirdesh jari kar rahe hai
 If the authorities do not follow his orders, he is even threatening them for transfer
 yah loktantr ke liye acha nahin he
 ' sisodiya ne kaha, 'hamane raashtrapati ko bataaya ki hamane kaaryvahak mukhya sachiv kii niyukti ke uparajyapal ke faisle ko aapas main salaah kiye bina sweekaar kar liya
 But even then he is ignoring the elected government and appointing officers
 vah yahaan tak ki sachivon kii niyuktiyon main hastkshep bhi kar rahe hai or unhen sidhe aadesh de rahe hai
 So where is democracy
 ' At the same time, Lieutenant Governor Najeeb Jung had also met Home Minister Rajnath Singh earlier in the day on this issue and gave information about his deadlock with AAP government
 shakuntla gamelin kii dilli kii kaaryvahak mukhya sachiv ke taur par niyukti ko lekar aap sarkaar or jang ke bich takaraav tej ho gaya he
 Kejriwal alleges that the Lieutenant Governor is trying to take over the administration
 kejariwal ke purajor virodh ke baavjood jang ne shuukravaar ko pad par gamelin kii niyukti kar di
 Describing the meeting with Mukherjee as good, Sisodia said, "we requested him to tell the Lieutenant Governor not to do what he is doing
" raashtrapati ne dhyaan se hamaari baat suni or mujhe ummid he ki vah is maamle main dekhenge
 'he said,' We told the President that the Lieutenant Governor is acting in such a way as to impose President's rule in Delhi
 mukhya baat he ki vah sidhe adhikariyon ko nirdesh de rahe hai
 In the last one week, he has ignored the Chief Minister, Ministers and Council of Ministers at least four times and ordered direct officers
 ' Earlier, the AAP government today appointed senior officer Arvind Rai as Principal Secretary, General Administration Department, ignoring the Lieutenant Governor
 gaur karne vaali baat he ki raay kii niyukti kaa aadesh rajendra kumaar ne pradhan sachiv (seva) kii haisiyat se jari kiya jabaki aap sarkaar dwaara is pad par kumaar kii niyukti ko jang ne kal nishprabhavi ghoshit kiya tha
 The AAP government handed over the responsibility of general administration department and service department from Anindo Majumdar to Kumar
 majumdaar ko shanivaar ko isliye hataa diya gaya, kyonki unhone shuukravaar ko kaaryvahak mukhya sachiv ke rup main shakuntla gamelin kii niyukti kii adhisuchana vaala aadesh jari kiya tha
 On the same day in the evening, the Lt
 Governor declared Mazumdar's transfer as 'ineffective'
 tippaniyan When Majumdar reached his office in Delhi Secretariat on Monday, the lock was hanging there
 baad main aap sarkaar ne kumaar ko seva or saamaanya prashasan vibhaag ke pradhan sachiv pad par baitha diya
 The AAP government today said in its order that Rai has been appointed Principal Secretary in place of Rajendra Kumar
 is saal kii shuruyaat main aap sarkaar ne raay ko grih vibhaag ke pradhan sachiv pad se hataaya tha or tab se unhen koi jimmedaari nahin saunpi
